  function insertAfter(newElement, referenceNode) {

      referenceNode.parentNode.insertBefore(newElement, referenceNode.nextSibling);

  }



  function marcarWhatsapp() {

      var width = screen.width;

      var device = '';

      if (width > 767) {

          device = 'Desktop';

      } else { 

          device = 'Mobile';

      }

      var url = document.URL;

      gtag('event', device, { 'event_category': 'Click botón Whatsapp', 'event_label': url, 'value': ''});

  }
